 (from input agencies) (input agenciyon se) Ajit Doval, who was the brain behind Balakot air strike and surgical strike and played a key role for Prime Minister Narendra Modi, has been appointed as the National Security Advisor of the country once again on Monday
 ajit dobhaal kii ye niyukti paanch saal kii hogi
 In the last 5 years, seeing the work of Ajit Doval, he has also been promoted
 rashtriya suraksha kshetra main achche kaam ke liye unhen cabinet mantri kaa darja mil gaya he
 Prior to this, he had the status of Minister of State
 cabinet kii niyukti samiti ne 31 may 2019 se prabhavi hone ke saath rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar ke rup main ajit dobhaal kii niyukti ko manjuuri de di he
 In 2014, Ajit Doval was appointed the fifth NSA of the country in the first term of the Modi government
 apane paanch saal ke pehle kaarykaal main ajit dobhaal ne safalataa kii kahaniyaan gadhi
 It started when he brought back 46 nurses trapped in a hospital in Iraq
 iske baad doklam vivaad ko sulajhane ke peeche bhi ajit dobhaal kaa hi dimag tha
 Apart from him, the credit was given to the then Foreign Secretary and the current Foreign Minister S
K
 jaishankar or china main bhartiya rajdoot vijay gokhale ko bhi diya jaataa he
 In October 2018, Ajit Doval was made the secretary of the Strategic Policy Group (strategic Policy Group, SPG) in addition to the NSA
 dobhaal piem modi ke sabase bharosmand naukarshah maane jate hai
 If in the last 5 years, the Indian Army entered into pok and did surgical strikes and air strikes in Balakot, then the credit also goes to Ajit Doval
 parde ke peeche rahakar kaam karne vaale is shaks ke netritv main hi bharat ne pakistan ko uski aukaat dikhaai
 Not only this, Ajit Doval played an important role in the release of Wing Commander Abhinandan from Pakistan after Balakot Airstrike
 1968 batch ke ipies adhikari dobhaal 2005 main intelligence beuro(ib) ke nideshak ke taur par ritair hue the
 a strategic thinker, Doval is the only police officer awarded the Kirti Chakra
 unhone mizoram, punjab, pakistan or united kingdom main seva kii he

 desh main sabase majboot naukarshah ke rup main unka udai is tathy se dekha ja saktaa he ki rashtriya suraksha parishad kii madad ke liye unhen espiji kaa sachiv banaaya gaya
 Earlier the cabinet secretary used to be its head

 Doval had to intervene when the government was not able to put forth its views on the Rafale case with clarity
